In June 2010 I watched Linus unbox a motherboard outside his workplace on a park bench holding a camera in his hand and recording  first person style.  I thought it was a woman unboxing because that's how his voice sounded to me. ğŸ˜‚. The next unboxing he did, he had a camera man now and he was onscreen. He was unboxing a Core i7 875k CPU.  That is the CPU that I bought after his unboxing to build my first Gaming Rig around. He eventually unboxed all the other components that I bought for my pc as well and I'm sure those unboxing videos still exist on channel; Asus P7P55D motherboard, Cooler master Silent Pro 1000W power Supply, the Hyper 212 cooler, the Antec 300 PC case, the MSI Cyclone GTX 460 graphics card that I eventually upgraded to a Cyclone 560 and then a Twin Frozr 660 and later a Twin Frozr RX 580. All reviewed and recommended by Linus.  I gamed on that PC for ten plus years until I got tired of having to switch GPUs constantly to keep up with newer games and decided to give console gaming a try by sticking with my PS4.
